remove_variable_warships = {
	event_target:global_event_country = {
		set_variable = {
			which = giga_ruined_warships_perc
			value = 100
		}
	}
}

remove_variable_player_megas = {
	event_target:global_event_country = {
		set_variable = {
			which = giga_mega_cost
			value = 100
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = giga_mega_output
			value = 100
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = giga_mega_upkeep
			value = 100
		}
	}
}
remove_variable_ai_megas = {
	event_target:global_event_country = {
		set_variable = {
			which = giga_mega_cost_ai
			value = 50
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = giga_mega_output_ai
			value = 100
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = giga_mega_upkeep_ai
			value = 100
		}
	}
}

remove_flags_scaling = {#Look into switching these to disabled for standardization purposes since as is they're only on when set whereas everything else is only OFF
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = has_real_space_mod }
		}
		remove_global_flag = giga_o_stars_disabled
	}
	set_global_flag = giga_dyson_scaling
	set_global_flag = giga_matroishka_scaling 
	set_global_flag = giga_lifter_scaling
}

remove_flags_achievements = {
	remove_global_flag = giga_achievements_disabled
	remove_global_flag = giga_achievements_effect_disabled
}

disable_menu_mega = { #relocated this here for ease of access and to keep it consistant
	set_global_flag = vanilla_dyson_disabled
	set_global_flag = vanilla_interstellar_disabled

# Blokkazoi
giga_preset_patreon_20 = {
	remove_all_menu_flags = yes
	remove_flags_buildcap = yes
	set_global_flag = giga_buildcap_1
	event_target:global_event_country = {
		set_variable = {
			which = giga_ruined_warships_perc
			value = 1
		}
	}
	disable_menu_mega = yes #Kazoi asked for all megas to be disabled, this was a simpler way of guaranteeing it into the future
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = giga_game_started
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = giga_blokkats_deathmode
		event_target:global_event_country = {
			set_variable = {
				which = blokkat_spawn_date
				value = 2200
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = giga_mega_output
				value = 10
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = giga_mega_output_ai
				value = 1000
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = giga_mega_cost
				value = 1000
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = giga_mega_cost_ai
				value = 10
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = giga_mega_upkeep
				value = 1000
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = giga_mega_upkeep_ai
				value = 10
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = giga_fe_planetcrafts_4
		set_global_flag = ehof_disabled
		set_global_flag = giga_dyson_scaling
		set_global_flag = giga_lifter_scaling
		set_global_flag = giga_matroishka_scaling
		set_global_flag = katzenartig_improbable
		set_global_flag = giga_jupitwo_disabled
		set_global_flag = giga_habitats_disabled
		set_global_flag = giga_gatzo_nopaluushia
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = sofe_activated
			}
			set_global_flag = giga_core_aeternum_4
		}
		else = {
			set_global_flag = giga_core_aeternum_3

		limit = {has_global_flag = asteroid_manufactory_capped_u}
		log = "set_global_flag = asteroid_manufactory_capped_u"
	} else = {
		log = "#No flag for Asteroid manufactory found!"
	}

	if = { # Psychic beacon
		limit = {has_global_flag = psychic_beacon_disabled}
		log = "set_global_flag = psychic_beacon_disabled"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = psychic_beacon_capped_1}
		log = "set_global_flag = psychic_beacon_capped_1"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = psychic_beacon_capped_2}
		log = "set_global_flag = psychic_beacon_capped_2"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = psychic_beacon_capped_3}
		log = "set_global_flag = psychic_beacon_capped_3"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = psychic_beacon_capped_r}
		log = "set_global_flag = psychic_beacon_capped_r"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = psychic_beacon_capped_u}
		log = "set_global_flag = psychic_beacon_capped_u"
	} else = {
		log = "#No flag for Psychic beacon found!"
	}

	if = { # Asteroid artillery
		limit = {has_global_flag = asteroid_artillery_disabled}
		log = "set_global_flag = asteroid_artillery_disabled"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = asteroid_artillery_capped_1}
		log = "set_global_flag = asteroid_artillery_capped_1"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = asteroid_artillery_capped_2}
		log = "set_global_flag = asteroid_artillery_capped_2"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = asteroid_artillery_capped_3}
		log = "set_global_flag = asteroid_artillery_capped_3"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = asteroid_artillery_capped_r}
		log = "set_global_flag = asteroid_artillery_capped_r"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = asteroid_artillery_capped_u}
		log = "set_global_flag = asteroid_artillery_capped_u"
	} else = {
		log = "#No flag for Asteroid Artillery found!"
	} 
	
	if = { # Builcap
		limit = {has_global_flag = giga_buildcap_1}
		log = "set_global_flag = giga_buildcap_1"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = giga_buildcap_2}
		log = "set_global_flag = giga_buildcap_2"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = giga_buildcap_3}
		log = "set_global_flag = giga_buildcap_3"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = giga_buildcap_u}
		log = "set_global_flag = giga_buildcap_u"
	} else_if = {
		limit = {has_global_flag = giga_buildcap_j}
		log = "set_global_flag = giga_buildcap_j"
	} else = {
		log = "#No flag for buildcap found!"
	}
	
	if = { # Habitats / elsyiums
		limit = {has_global_flag = giga_habitats_disabled}
		log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_disabled"
	} 
	# else_if = { Deprecated
	# 	limit = {has_global_flag = giga_habitats_unlimited}
	# 	log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_unlimited"
	# } else_if = {
	# 	limit = {has_global_flag = giga_habitats_system_3}
	# 	log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_system_3"
	# 	log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_system"
	# } else_if = {
	# 	limit = {has_global_flag = giga_habitats_system_10}
	# 	log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_system_10"
	# 	log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_system"
	# } else_if = {
	# 	limit = {has_global_flag = giga_habitats_system_25}
	# 	log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_system_25"
	# 	log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_system"
	# } else_if = {
	# 	limit = {has_global_flag = giga_habitats_pop_25}
	# 	log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_pop_25"
	# 	log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_pop"
	# } else_if = {
	# 	limit = {has_global_flag = giga_habitats_pop_50}
	# 	log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_pop_50"
	# 	log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_pop"
	# } else_if = {
	# 	limit = {has_global_flag = giga_habitats_pop_100}
	# 	log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_pop_100"
	# 	log = "set_global_flag = giga_habitats_pop"
	# } 
	else = {
		log = "#No flag for habitats found! Assume Enabled"
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = giga_habitats_advanced_orbitals_disabled }
		log = "set_globlal_flag = giga_habitats_advanced_orbitals_disabled"
	}else = {
		log = "#No flag for advanced orbitals found! Assume Enabled"
	}

	# log = "----------------------------------------------------------------------------"
	log = "event_target:global_event_country = { set_variable = { which = giga_ruined_warships_perc value = \\[global_event_country.giga_ruined_warships_perc] }"
	# log = "Wrecked Warship Amount = \\[global_event_country.giga_ruined_warships_perc]"
	if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				is_variable_set = blokkat_spawn_date
			}
		}
		log = "set_variable = { which = blokkat_spawn_date value = \\[global_event_country.blokkat_spawn_date]  }"
		# log = "Blokkat Spawn Date = \\[global_event_country.blokkat_spawn_date]"
	} else = { #Defaults the blokkat start date
		log = "set_variable = {which = blokkat_spawn_date value = 2500}"
	}
	event_target:global_event_country = {
		log = "set_variable = { which = giga_mega_output value = \\[this.giga_mega_output]  }"
		log = "set_variable = { which = giga_mega_output_ai value = \\[this.giga_mega_output_ai]  }"
		log = "set_variable = { which = giga_mega_cost value = \\[this.giga_mega_cost]  }"
		log = "set_variable = { which = giga_mega_cost_ai value = \\[this.giga_mega_cost_ai]  }"
		log = "set_variable = { which = giga_mega_upkeep value = \\[this.giga_mega_upkeep]  }"
		log = "set_variable = { which = giga_mega_upkeep_ai value = \\[this.giga_mega_upkeep_ai]  }"
		log = "}"
		# log = "Giga Mega Output = \\[this.giga_mega_output]"
		# log = "Giga Mega Output AI = \\[this.giga_mega_output_ai]"
		# log = "Giga Mega Cost = \\[this.giga_mega_cost]"
		# log = "Giga Mega Cost AI = \\[this.giga_mega_cost_ai]"
		# log = "Giga Mega Upkeep = \\[this.giga_mega_upkeep]"
		# log = "Giga Mega Upkeep AI = \\[this.giga_mega_upkeep_ai]"
	}
	log = "_________________________________________________________________________"
	log = "_________________________________________________________________________"
}
